SELECT [s1].[Id], [s1].[Current], [s1].[DeviceId], [s1].[PowerConsumptionKW], [s1].[Temperature], [s1].[Timestamp], [s1].[Voltage]
FROM (
    SELECT [d].[IsActive]
    FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e]
    INNER JOIN [Devices] AS [d] ON [e].[DeviceId] = [d].[Id]
    WHERE [e].[Timestamp] >= DATEADD(minute, CAST(-5.0E0 AS int), GETUTCDATE())
    GROUP BY [d].[IsActive]
) AS [s]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s0].[Id], [s0].[Current], [s0].[DeviceId], [s0].[PowerConsumptionKW], [s0].[Temperature], [s0].[Timestamp], [s0].[Voltage], [s0].[IsActive]
    FROM (
        SELECT [e0].[Id], [e0].[Current], [e0].[DeviceId], [e0].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e0].[Temperature], [e0].[Timestamp], [e0].[Voltage], [d0].[IsActive], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [d0].[IsActive] ORDER BY [e0].[Timestamp] DESC) AS [row]
        FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e0]
        INNER JOIN [Devices] AS [d0] ON [e0].[DeviceId] = [d0].[Id]
        WHERE [e0].[Timestamp] >= DATEADD(minute, CAST(-5.0E0 AS int), GETUTCDATE())
    ) AS [s0]
    WHERE [s0].[row] <= 1
) AS [s1] ON [s].[IsActive] = [s1].[IsActive]

FROM (
    SELECT [d].[IsActive]
    FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e]
    INNER JOIN [Devices] AS [d] ON [e].[DeviceId] = [d].[Id]
    WHERE [e].[Timestamp] >= DATEADD(minute, CAST(-5.0E0 AS int), GETUTCDATE())
    GROUP BY [d].[IsActive]
) AS [s]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s0].[Id], [s0].[Current], [s0].[DeviceId], [s0].[PowerConsumptionKW], [s0].[Temperature], [s0].[Timestamp], [s0].[Voltage], [s0].[IsActive]
    FROM (
        SELECT [e0].[Id], [e0].[Current], [e0].[DeviceId], [e0].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e0].[Temperature], [e0].[Timestamp], [e0].[Voltage], [d0].[IsActive], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [d0].[IsActive] ORDER BY [e0].[Timestamp] DESC) AS [row]
        FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e0]
        INNER JOIN [Devices] AS [d0] ON [e0].[DeviceId] = [d0].[Id]
        WHERE [e0].[Timestamp] >= DATEADD(minute, CAST(-5.0E0 AS int), GETUTCDATE())
    ) AS [s0]
    WHERE [s0].[row] <= 1
) AS [s1] ON [s].[IsActive] = [s1].[IsActive]

SELECT [e].[Timestamp], [d].[Name], CASE [d].[Type]
    WHEN 1 THEN N'AirConditioner'
    WHEN 2 THEN N'Refrigerator'
    WHEN 3 THEN N'WashingMachine'
    WHEN 4 THEN N'WaterHeater'
    WHEN 5 THEN N'Lights'
    WHEN 6 THEN N'TV'
    WHEN 7 THEN N'Microwave'
    WHEN 99 THEN N'Other'
    ELSE CAST([d].[Type] AS nvarchar(max))
END, [z].[Name], [e].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e].[Voltage], [e].[Current], [e].[Temperature]
FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e]
INNER JOIN [Devices] AS [d] ON [e].[DeviceId] = [d].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Zones] AS [z] ON [d].[ZoneId] = [z].[Id]
WHERE [e].[Timestamp] >= @__start_0 AND [e].[Timestamp] <= @__end_1 AND [e].[DeviceId] = @__deviceId_Value_2
ORDER BY [e].[Timestamp]
